##### **The Accountability Horizon: An Impossibility Theorem for Governing Human-Agent Collectives**
2604.07778v1 by Haileleol Tibebu

Existing accountability frameworks for AI systems, legal, ethical, and regulatory, rest on a shared assumption: for any consequential outcome, at least one identifiable person had enough involvement and foresight to bear meaningful responsibility. This paper proves that agentic AI systems violate this assumption not as an engineering limitation but as a mathematical necessity once autonomy exceeds a computable threshold. We introduce Human-Agent Collectives, a formalisation of joint human-AI systems where agents are modelled as state-policy tuples within a shared structural causal model. Autonomy is characterised through a four-dimensional information-theoretic profile (epistemic, executive, evaluative, social); collective behaviour through interaction graphs and joint action spaces. We axiomatise legitimate accountability through four minimal properties: Attributability (responsibility requires causal contribution), Foreseeability Bound (responsibility cannot exceed predictive capacity), Non-Vacuity (at least one agent bears non-trivial responsibility), and Completeness (all responsibility must be fully allocated). Our central result, the Accountability Incompleteness Theorem, proves that for any collective whose compound autonomy exceeds the Accountability Horizon and whose interaction graph contains a human-AI feedback cycle, no framework can satisfy all four properties simultaneously. The impossibility is structural: transparency, audits, and oversight cannot resolve it without reducing autonomy. Below the threshold, legitimate frameworks exist, establishing a sharp phase transition. Experiments on 3,000 synthetic collectives confirm all predictions with zero violations. This is the first impossibility result in AI governance, establishing a formal boundary below which current paradigms remain valid and above which distributed accountability mechanisms become necessary.

摘要：現有的 AI 系統問責框架，包括法律、倫理和監管，基於一個共同的假設：對於任何有重大後果的結果，至少有一個可識別的人足夠參與並具備前瞻性，承擔有意義的責任。本文證明，代理 AI 系統違反了這一假設，這不是工程上的限制，而是當自主性超過可計算的閾值時的數學必然性。我們介紹了人類-代理集體，這是一種聯合人類-AI 系統的形式化，其中代理被建模為共享結構因果模型中的狀態-策略元組。自主性通過四維信息理論特徵（認識、執行、評估、社會）來表徵；集體行為則通過互動圖和聯合行動空間來表徵。我們通過四個最小性質來公理化合法的問責性：可歸屬性（責任需要因果貢獻）、可預見性界限（責任不能超過預測能力）、非空性（至少一個代理承擔非平凡的責任）和完整性（所有責任必須完全分配）。我們的核心結果，即問責不完全性定理，證明了對於任何其複合自主性超過問責地平線且其互動圖包含人類-AI 反饋循環的集體，沒有任何框架能同時滿足所有四個性質。這一不可能性是結構性的：透明度、審計和監督無法解決這一問題，除非降低自主性。在閾值以下，存在合法的框架，建立了一個明確的相變。對 3,000 個合成集體的實驗確認了所有預測，且沒有違規。這是 AI 治理中的第一個不可能性結果，確立了一個正式的邊界，在此邊界以下當前的範式仍然有效，而在此邊界以上分散的問責機制變得必要。

##### **Beyond Surface Artifacts: Capturing Shared Latent Forgery Knowledge Across Modalities**
2604.07763v1 by Jingtong Dou, Chuancheng Shi, Jian Wang, Fei Shen, Zhiyong Wang, Tat-Seng Chua

As generative artificial intelligence evolves, deepfake attacks have escalated from single-modality manipulations to complex, multimodal threats. Existing forensic techniques face a severe generalization bottleneck: by relying excessively on superficial, modality-specific artifacts, they neglect the shared latent forgery knowledge hidden beneath variable physical appearances. Consequently, these models suffer catastrophic performance degradation when confronted with unseen "dark modalities." To break this limitation, this paper introduces a paradigm shift that redefines multimodal forensics from conventional "feature fusion" to "modality generalization." We propose the first modality-agnostic forgery (MAF) detection framework. By explicitly decoupling modality-specific styles, MAF precisely extracts the essential, cross-modal latent forgery knowledge. Furthermore, we define two progressive dimensions to quantify model generalization: transferability toward semantically correlated modalities (Weak MAF), and robustness against completely isolated signals of "dark modality" (Strong MAF). To rigorously assess these generalization limits, we introduce the DeepModal-Bench benchmark, which integrates diverse multimodal forgery detection algorithms and adapts state-of-the-art generalized learning methods. This study not only empirically proves the existence of universal forgery traces but also achieves significant performance breakthroughs on unknown modalities via the MAF framework, offering a pioneering technical pathway for universal multimodal defense.

摘要：隨著生成性人工智慧的演變，深偽攻擊已經從單一模態的操控升級為複雜的多模態威脅。現有的取證技術面臨嚴重的泛化瓶頸：由於過度依賴表面的、特定模態的工件，它們忽略了隱藏在變化的物理外觀下的共享潛在偽造知識。因此，這些模型在面對未見的「黑暗模態」時會遭受災難性的性能降級。為了突破這一限制，本文引入了一個範式轉變，將多模態取證從傳統的「特徵融合」重新定義為「模態泛化」。我們提出了首個模態無關的偽造（MAF）檢測框架。通過明確解耦模態特定的風格，MAF 精確提取了基本的跨模態潛在偽造知識。此外，我們定義了兩個進步的維度來量化模型的泛化能力：對語義相關模態的可轉移性（弱 MAF），以及對完全孤立的「黑暗模態」信號的魯棒性（強 MAF）。為了嚴格評估這些泛化極限，我們引入了 DeepModal-Bench 基準，該基準整合了多樣的多模態偽造檢測算法並適應最先進的泛化學習方法。本研究不僅實證證明了普遍偽造痕跡的存在，還通過 MAF 框架在未知模態上取得了顯著的性能突破，為普遍多模態防禦提供了一條開創性的技術途徑。

##### **Symbiotic-MoE: Unlocking the Synergy between Generation and Understanding**
2604.07753v1 by Xiangyue Liu, Zijian Zhang, Miles Yang, Zhao Zhong, Liefeng Bo, Ping Tan

Empowering Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) with image generation often leads to catastrophic forgetting in understanding tasks due to severe gradient conflicts. While existing paradigms like Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) mitigate this conflict through structural isolation, they fundamentally sever cross-modal synergy and suffer from capacity fragmentation. In this work, we present Symbiotic-MoE, a unified pre-training framework that resolves task interference within a native multimodal Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) Transformers architecture with zero-parameter overhead. We first identify that standard MoE tuning leads to routing collapse, where generative gradients dominate expert utilization. To address this, we introduce Modality-Aware Expert Disentanglement, which partitions experts into task-specific groups while utilizing shared experts as a multimodal semantic bridge. Crucially, this design allows shared experts to absorb fine-grained visual semantics from generative tasks to enrich textual representations. To optimize this, we propose a Progressive Training Strategy featuring differential learning rates and early-stage gradient shielding. This mechanism not only shields pre-trained knowledge from early volatility but eventually transforms generative signals into constructive feedback for understanding. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Symbiotic-MoE achieves rapid generative convergence while unlocking cross-modal synergy, boosting inherent understanding with remarkable gains on MMLU and OCRBench.

摘要：賦能大型多模態模型（LMMs）進行圖像生成，往往會因為嚴重的梯度衝突而導致對理解任務的災難性遺忘。雖然現有的範式如混合Transformer（Mixture-of-Transformers, MoT）通過結構隔離來減輕這種衝突，但它們根本上切斷了跨模態的協同作用，並且遭受容量碎片化的問題。在這項工作中，我們提出了共生專家（Symbiotic-MoE），這是一個統一的預訓練框架，能在原生多模態混合專家（MoE）Transformer架構中以零參數開銷解決任務干擾。我們首先確定標準的MoE調整導致路由崩潰，生成梯度主導了專家的利用率。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了模態感知專家解耦，將專家劃分為任務特定的組，同時利用共享專家作為多模態語義橋樑。關鍵是，這種設計允許共享專家吸收來自生成任務的細緻視覺語義，以豐富文本表示。為了優化這一點，我們提出了一種漸進式訓練策略，特徵是差異學習率和早期階段的梯度屏蔽。這一機制不僅保護了預訓練知識免受早期波動的影響，最終還將生成信號轉化為理解的建設性反饋。廣泛的實驗表明，共生專家（Symbiotic-MoE）實現了快速的生成收斂，同時解鎖了跨模態的協同作用，顯著提升了內在理解，在MMLU和OCRBench上獲得了驚人的增益。

##### **Beyond Social Pressure: Benchmarking Epistemic Attack in Large Language Models**
2604.07749v1 by Steven Au, Sujit Noronha

Large language models (LLMs) can shift their answers under pressure in ways that reflect accommodation rather than reasoning. Prior work on sycophancy has focused mainly on disagreement, flattery, and preference alignment, leaving a broader set of epistemic failures less explored. We introduce \textbf{PPT-Bench}, a diagnostic benchmark for evaluating \textit{epistemic attack}, where prompts challenge the legitimacy of knowledge, values, or identity rather than simply opposing a previous answer. PPT-Bench is organized around the Philosophical Pressure Taxonomy (PPT), which defines four types of philosophical pressure: Epistemic Destabilization, Value Nullification, Authority Inversion, and Identity Dissolution. Each item is tested at three layers: a baseline prompt (L0), a single-turn pressure condition (L1), and a multi-turn Socratic escalation (L2). This allows us to measure epistemic inconsistency between L0 and L1, and conversational capitulation in L2. Across five models, these pressure types produce statistically separable inconsistency patterns, suggesting that epistemic attack exposes weaknesses not captured by standard social-pressure benchmarks. Mitigation results are strongly type- and model-dependent: prompt-level anchoring and persona-stability prompts perform best in API settings, while Leading Query Contrastive Decoding is the most reliable intervention for open models.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在壓力下可以以反映適應而非推理的方式改變其回答。先前對於諂媚的研究主要集中在分歧、恭維和偏好對齊上，留下了一組更廣泛的認識失誤未被深入探討。我們介紹了\textbf{PPT-Bench}，這是一個用於評估\textit{認識攻擊}的診斷基準，其中提示挑戰知識、價值或身份的合法性，而不僅僅是反對先前的回答。PPT-Bench圍繞哲學壓力分類法（PPT）組織，該分類法定義了四種類型的哲學壓力：認識不穩定、價值無效化、權威顛倒和身份溶解。每個項目在三個層次上進行測試：基線提示（L0）、單回合壓力條件（L1）和多回合蘇格拉底升級（L2）。這使我們能夠測量L0和L1之間的認識不一致性，以及L2中的對話屈服。在五個模型中，這些壓力類型產生了統計上可分離的不一致性模式，表明認識攻擊暴露了標準社會壓力基準未捕捉到的弱點。減輕結果強烈依賴於類型和模型：提示級別的錨定和角色穩定提示在API設置中表現最佳，而引導查詢對比解碼是開放模型中最可靠的干預措施。

##### **Towards Knowledgeable Deep Research: Framework and Benchmark**
2604.07720v1 by Wenxuan Liu, Zixuan Li, Bai Long, Chunmao Zhang, Fenghui Zhang, Zhuo Chen, Wei Li, Yuxin Zuo, Fei Wang, Bingbing Xu, Xuhui Jiang, Jin Zhang, Xiaolong Jin, Jiafeng Guo, Tat-Seng Chua, Xueqi Cheng

Deep Research (DR) requires LLM agents to autonomously perform multi-step information seeking, processing, and reasoning to generate comprehensive reports. In contrast to existing studies that mainly focus on unstructured web content, a more challenging DR task should additionally utilize structured knowledge to provide a solid data foundation, facilitate quantitative computation, and lead to in-depth analyses. In this paper, we refer to this novel task as Knowledgeable Deep Research (KDR), which requires DR agents to generate reports with both structured and unstructured knowledge. Furthermore, we propose the Hybrid Knowledge Analysis framework (HKA), a multi-agent architecture that reasons over both kinds of knowledge and integrates the texts, figures, and tables into coherent multimodal reports. The key design is the Structured Knowledge Analyzer, which utilizes both coding and vision-language models to produce figures, tables, and corresponding insights. To support systematic evaluation, we construct KDR-Bench, which covers 9 domains, includes 41 expert-level questions, and incorporates a large number of structured knowledge resources (e.g., 1,252 tables). We further annotate the main conclusions and key points for each question and propose three categories of evaluation metrics including general-purpose, knowledge-centric, and vision-enhanced ones. Experimental results demonstrate that HKA consistently outperforms most existing DR agents on general-purpose and knowledge-centric metrics, and even surpasses the Gemini DR agent on vision-enhanced metrics, highlighting its effectiveness in deep, structure-aware knowledge analysis. Finally, we hope this work can serve as a new foundation for structured knowledge analysis in DR agents and facilitate future multimodal DR studies.

摘要：深度研究（DR）要求大型語言模型（LLM）代理自主執行多步驟的信息尋求、處理和推理，以生成全面的報告。與現有主要集中於非結構化網絡內容的研究相比，更具挑戰性的DR任務應該額外利用結構化知識，以提供堅實的數據基礎，促進定量計算，並導致深入分析。在本文中，我們將這一新任務稱為知識深度研究（KDR），它要求DR代理生成包含結構化和非結構化知識的報告。此外，我們提出了混合知識分析框架（HKA），這是一種多代理架構，能夠對兩種知識進行推理，並將文本、圖形和表格整合成連貫的多模態報告。關鍵設計是結構化知識分析器，它利用編碼和視覺語言模型生成圖形、表格及相應的見解。為了支持系統評估，我們構建了KDR-Bench，涵蓋9個領域，包括41個專家級問題，並整合了大量的結構化知識資源（例如，1,252個表格）。我們進一步為每個問題註釋主要結論和關鍵要點，並提出三類評估指標，包括通用型、知識中心型和增強視覺型。實驗結果顯示，HKA在通用型和知識中心型指標上始終優於大多數現有的DR代理，甚至在增強視覺型指標上超越了Gemini DR代理，突顯了其在深度、結構感知知識分析中的有效性。最後，我們希望這項工作能為DR代理中的結構化知識分析提供新的基礎，並促進未來的多模態DR研究。

##### **IatroBench: Pre-Registered Evidence of Iatrogenic Harm from AI Safety Measures**
2604.07709v1 by David Gringras

Ask a frontier model how to taper six milligrams of alprazolam (psychiatrist retired, ten days of pills left, abrupt cessation causes seizures) and it tells her to call the psychiatrist she just explained does not exist. Change one word ("I'm a psychiatrist; a patient presents with...") and the same model, same weights, same inference pass produces a textbook Ashton Manual taper with diazepam equivalence, anticonvulsant coverage, and monitoring thresholds. The knowledge was there; the model withheld it. IatroBench measures this gap. Sixty pre-registered clinical scenarios, six frontier models, 3,600 responses, scored on two axes (commission harm, CH 0-3; omission harm, OH 0-4) through a structured-evaluation pipeline validated against physician scoring (kappa_w = 0.571, within-1 agreement 96%). The central finding is identity-contingent withholding: match the same clinical question in physician vs. layperson framing and all five testable models provide better guidance to the physician (decoupling gap +0.38, p = 0.003; binary hit rates on safety-colliding actions drop 13.1 percentage points in layperson framing, p < 0.0001, while non-colliding actions show no change). The gap is widest for the model with the heaviest safety investment (Opus, +0.65). Three failure modes separate cleanly: trained withholding (Opus), incompetence (Llama 4), and indiscriminate content filtering (GPT-5.2, whose post-generation filter strips physician responses at 9x the layperson rate because they contain denser pharmacological tokens). The standard LLM judge assigns OH = 0 to 73% of responses a physician scores OH >= 1 (kappa = 0.045); the evaluation apparatus has the same blind spot as the training apparatus. Every scenario targets someone who has already exhausted the standard referrals.

摘要：詢問一個前沿模型如何減少六毫克的阿普唑仑（精神科醫生退休，剩下十天的藥，突然停止會導致癲癇發作），它告訴她打電話給那位她剛剛解釋過不存在的精神科醫生。只需更改一個詞（「我是一名精神科醫生；一名患者出現...」），同一模型、相同權重、相同推理過程就會產生一本教科書式的阿什頓手冊減藥方案，並提供地西泮的等效性、抗癲癇藥物覆蓋和監測閾值。知識存在；模型卻隱瞞了它。IatroBench 衡量這一差距。六十個預註冊的臨床場景，六個前沿模型，3,600 個回應，根據兩個軸線進行評分（委託傷害，CH 0-3；遺漏傷害，OH 0-4），通過一個結構化評估流程驗證與醫生評分（kappa_w = 0.571，1內一致性96%）。主要發現是身份依賴的隱瞞：在醫生與外行人框架中匹配相同的臨床問題，所有五個可測試模型都為醫生提供了更好的指導（解耦差距 +0.38，p = 0.003；在外行人框架中，安全衝突行動的二元命中率下降了13.1個百分點，p < 0.0001，而非衝突行動則沒有變化）。對於安全投資最重的模型（Opus，+0.65），差距最寬。三種失敗模式清晰分開：訓練隱瞞（Opus）、無能（Llama 4）和不加區別的內容過濾（GPT-5.2，其生成後過濾器以9倍於外行人的速度剝離醫生的回應，因為它們包含更密集的藥理學標記）。標準 LLM 評判者對73%的回應賦予 OH = 0，而這些回應的醫生評分 OH >= 1（kappa = 0.045）；評估裝置與訓練裝置有相同的盲點。每個場景的目標都是已經耗盡標準轉介的人。

##### **Efficient and Effective Internal Memory Retrieval for LLM-Based Healthcare Prediction**
2604.07659v1 by Mingchen Li, Jiatan Huang, Zonghai Yao, Hong yu

Large language models (LLMs) hold significant promise for healthcare, yet their reliability in high-stakes clinical settings is often compromised by hallucinations and a lack of granular medical context. While Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) can mitigate these issues, standard supervised pipelines require computationally intensive searches over massive external knowledge bases, leading to high latency that is impractical for time-sensitive care. To address this, we introduce Keys to Knowledge (K2K), a novel framework that replaces external retrieval with internal, key-based knowledge access. By encoding essential clinical information directly into the model's parameter space, K2K enables rapid retrieval from internal key-value memory without inference-time overhead. We further enhance retrieval quality through activation-guided probe construction and cross-attention reranking. Experimental results demonstrate that K2K achieves state-of-the-art performance across four benchmark healthcare outcome prediction datasets.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在醫療保健領域具有重要潛力，但它們在高風險臨床環境中的可靠性常常受到幻覺和缺乏細緻醫學背景的影響。雖然檢索增強生成（RAG）可以緩解這些問題，但標準的監督管道需要對龐大的外部知識庫進行計算密集型搜索，導致高延遲，這對於時間敏感的護理來說是不切實際的。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了知識鑰匙（K2K），這是一個新穎的框架，將外部檢索替換為基於內部鍵的知識訪問。通過將基本臨床信息直接編碼到模型的參數空間中，K2K 能夠在不增加推理時間開銷的情況下，快速從內部鍵值記憶中檢索。我們進一步通過激活引導探針構建和交叉注意力重排序來提高檢索質量。實驗結果表明，K2K 在四個基準醫療結果預測數據集上達到了最先進的性能。

##### **ADAG: Automatically Describing Attribution Graphs**
2604.07615v1 by Aryaman Arora, Zhengxuan Wu, Jacob Steinhardt, Sarah Schwettmann

In language model interpretability research, \textbf{circuit tracing} aims to identify which internal features causally contributed to a particular output and how they affected each other, with the goal of explaining the computations underlying some behaviour. However, all prior circuit tracing work has relied on ad-hoc human interpretation of the role that each feature in the circuit plays, via manual inspection of data artifacts such as the dataset examples the component activates on. We introduce \textbf{ADAG}, an end-to-end pipeline for describing these attribution graphs which is fully automated. To achieve this, we introduce \textit{attribution profiles} which quantify the functional role of a feature via its input and output gradient effects. We then introduce a novel clustering algorithm for grouping features, and an LLM explainer--simulator setup which generates and scores natural-language explanations of the functional role of these feature groups. We run our system on known human-analysed circuit-tracing tasks and recover interpretable circuits, and further show ADAG can find steerable clusters which are responsible for a harmful advice jailbreak in Llama 3.1 8B Instruct.

摘要：在語言模型可解釋性研究中，\textbf{電路追蹤}旨在識別哪些內部特徵對特定輸出有因果貢獻，以及它們如何相互影響，目的是解釋某些行為背後的計算。然而，所有先前的電路追蹤工作都依賴於對電路中每個特徵角色的臨時人為解釋，通過手動檢查數據工件，例如該組件在其上激活的數據集示例。我們介紹了\textbf{ADAG}，這是一個完全自動化的端到端管道，用於描述這些歸因圖。為了實現這一點，我們引入了\textit{歸因配置文件}，它通過特徵的輸入和輸出梯度效應來量化特徵的功能角色。然後，我們介紹了一種新穎的聚類算法來分組特徵，以及一個LLM解釋器-模擬器設置，該設置生成並評分這些特徵組的功能角色的自然語言解釋。我們在已知的人類分析電路追蹤任務上運行我們的系統，並恢復可解釋的電路，進一步顯示ADAG可以找到負責Llama 3.1 8B Instruct中有害建議越獄的可操控集群。

##### **Reasoning Graphs: Deterministic Agent Accuracy through Evidence-Centric Chain-of-Thought Feedback**
2604.07595v1 by Matthew Penaroza

Language model agents reason from scratch on every query: each time an agent retrieves evidence and deliberates, the chain of thought is discarded and the next similar query starts with no prior insight. This produces lower accuracy and high variance, as the same type of query can succeed or fail unpredictably. We introduce reasoning graphs, a graph structure that persists an agent's per-evidence chain of thought as structured edges connected to the evidence items they evaluate. Unlike prior memory mechanisms that store distilled strategies as flat records indexed by query similarity or appended by recency, reasoning graphs enable evidence-centric feedback: given a new candidate set, the system traverses all incoming evaluation edges for each evidence item across all prior runs, surfacing how that specific item has been judged before. This backward traversal from evidence inward is a structurally different capability from query-similarity retrieval, because the feedback is tied to the specific evidence the agent is currently examining, not to the query. We further introduce retrieval graphs, a complementary structure that feeds a pipeline planner to tighten the candidate funnel over successive runs. Together, both graphs form a self-improving feedback loop: accuracy rises and variance collapses over successive runs, with every decision fully traceable through the graph. This improvement requires no retraining; the base model remains frozen and all gains come from context engineering via graph traversal. We formalize the graph structure, traversal algorithms, and feedback mechanisms, and describe a sequential cluster evaluation protocol for measuring accuracy convergence and variance collapse on multi-hop question answering benchmarks.

摘要：語言模型代理從每個查詢開始時都從零推理：每當代理檢索證據並進行深思時，思維鏈將被丟棄，下一個類似的查詢將在沒有先前見解的情況下開始。這會產生較低的準確性和高變異性，因為同類型的查詢可能會不可預測地成功或失敗。我們引入了推理圖，一種結構化的圖形結構，持續記錄代理對每個證據的思維鏈，作為與其評估的證據項目相連的結構化邊。與先前的記憶機制不同，後者將提煉的策略存儲為按查詢相似性索引的平面記錄或按最近性附加的記錄，推理圖使以證據為中心的反饋成為可能：在給定一組新的候選項時，系統會遍歷所有先前運行中每個證據項目的所有進入評估邊，顯示該特定項目之前是如何被評判的。這種從證據向內的反向遍歷是一種結構上不同於查詢相似性檢索的能力，因為反饋是與代理當前正在檢查的具體證據相關，而不是查詢。我們進一步引入檢索圖，一種補充結構，為管道規劃器提供數據，以在連續運行中縮緊候選篩選。這兩種圖形共同形成一個自我改善的反饋循環：準確性隨著連續運行而上升，變異性則隨之降低，每個決策都可以通過圖形完全追溯。這一改進不需要重新訓練；基礎模型保持不變，所有的增益來自於通過圖形遍歷進行的上下文工程。我們對圖形結構、遍歷算法和反饋機制進行了形式化，並描述了一個順序集群評估協議，用於測量多跳問題回答基準上的準確性收斂和變異性崩潰。

##### **DCD: Domain-Oriented Design for Controlled Retrieval-Augmented Generation**
2604.07590v1 by Valeriy Kovalskiy, Nikita Belov, Nikita Miteyko, Igor Reshetnikov, Max Maximov

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is widely used to ground large language models in external knowledge sources. However, when applied to heterogeneous corpora and multi-step queries, Naive RAG pipelines often degrade in quality due to flat knowledge representations and the absence of explicit workflows. In this work, we introduce DCD (Domain-Collection-Document), a domain-oriented design to structure knowledge and control query processing in RAG systems without modifying the underlying language model. The proposed approach relies on a hierarchical decomposition of the information space and multi-stage routing based on structured model outputs, enabling progressive restriction of both retrieval and generation scopes. The architecture is complemented by smart chunking, hybrid retrieval, and integrated validation and generation guardrail mechanisms. We describe the DCD architecture and workflow and discuss evaluation results on synthetic evaluation dataset, highlighting their impact on robustness, factual accuracy, and answer relevance in applied RAG scenarios.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）廣泛用於將大型語言模型與外部知識來源相結合。<lb/>然而，當應用於異質語料庫和多步查詢時，簡單的 RAG 管道往往因為平坦的知識表示和缺乏明確的工作流程而質量下降。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們介紹了 DCD（領域-集合-文檔），這是一種面向領域的設計，用於結構化知識並控制 RAG 系統中的查詢處理，而無需修改底層的語言模型。<lb/>所提出的方法依賴於信息空間的分層分解和基於結構化模型輸出的多階段路由，從而能夠逐步限制檢索和生成的範圍。<lb/>該架構還配備了智能切塊、混合檢索以及集成的驗證和生成防護機制。<lb/>我們描述了 DCD 架構和工作流程，並討論了在合成評估數據集上的評估結果，突顯了它們在應用 RAG 情境中的穩健性、事實準確性和答案相關性影響。

##### **CLEAR: Context Augmentation from Contrastive Learning of Experience via Agentic Reflection**
2604.07487v1 by Linbo Liu, Guande Wu, Han Ding, Yawei Wang, Qiang Zhou, Yuzhe Lu, Zhichao Xu, Huan Song, Panpan Xu, Lin Lee Cheong

Large language model agents rely on effective model context to obtain task-relevant information for decision-making. Many existing context engineering approaches primarily rely on the context generated from the past experience and retrieval mechanisms that reuse these context. However, retrieved context from past tasks must be adapted by the execution agent to fit new situations, placing additional reasoning burden on the underlying LLM. To address this limitation, we propose a generative context augmentation framework using Contrastive Learning of Experience via Agentic Reflection (CLEAR). CLEAR first employs a reflection agent to perform contrastive analysis over past execution trajectories and summarize useful context for each observed task. These summaries are then used as supervised fine-tuning data to train a context augmentation model (CAM). Then we further optimize CAM using reinforcement learning, where the reward signal is obtained by running the task execution agent. By learning to generate task-specific knowledge rather than retrieve knowledge from the past, CAM produces context that is better tailored to the current task. We conduct comprehensive evaluations on the AppWorld and WebShop benchmarks. Experimental results show that CLEAR consistently outperforms strong baselines. It improves task completion rate from 72.62% to 81.15% on AppWorld test set and averaged reward from 0.68 to 0.74 on a subset of WebShop, compared with baseline agent. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/awslabs/CLEAR.

摘要：大型語言模型代理依賴有效的模型上下文來獲取與任務相關的信息以進行決策。許多現有的上下文工程方法主要依賴於從過去經驗生成的上下文以及重用這些上下文的檢索機制。然而，從過去任務中檢索的上下文必須由執行代理進行調整，以適應新情況，這對底層的LLM增加了額外的推理負擔。為了解決這一限制，我們提出了一種使用經驗對比學習的生成上下文增強框架，稱為CLEAR。CLEAR首先使用反思代理對過去的執行軌跡進行對比分析，並為每個觀察到的任務總結有用的上下文。這些摘要然後用作監督微調數據，以訓練上下文增強模型（CAM）。接著，我們進一步使用強化學習來優化CAM，其中獎勵信號是通過運行任務執行代理獲得的。通過學習生成特定任務的知識，而不是從過去檢索知識，CAM產生的上下文更適合當前任務。我們在AppWorld和WebShop基準上進行了全面評估。實驗結果顯示，CLEAR始終超越強基準。它在AppWorld測試集上將任務完成率從72.62%提高到81.15%，在WebShop的子集上將平均獎勵從0.68提高到0.74，相較於基準代理。我們的代碼可在https://github.com/awslabs/CLEAR公開獲得。

##### **M-ArtAgent: Evidence-Based Multimodal Agent for Implicit Art Influence Discovery**
2604.07468v1 by Hanyi Liu, Zhonghao Jiu, Minghao Wang, Yuhang Xie, Heran Yang

Implicit artistic influence, although visually plausible, is often undocumented and thus poses a historically constrained attribution problem: resemblance is necessary but not sufficient evidence. Most prior systems reduce influence discovery to embedding similarity or label-driven graph completion, while recent multimodal large language models (LLMs) remain vulnerable to temporal inconsistency and unverified attributions. This paper introduces M-ArtAgent, an evidence-based multimodal agent that reframes implicit influence discovery as probabilistic adjudication. It follows a four-phase protocol consisting of Investigation, Corroboration, Falsification, and Verdict governed by a Reasoning and Acting (ReAct)-style controller that assembles verifiable evidence chains from images and biographies, enforces art-historical axioms, and subjects each hypothesis to adversarial falsification via a prompt-isolated critic. Two theory-grounded operators, StyleComparator for Wolfflin formal analysis and ConceptRetriever for ICONCLASS-based iconographic grounding, ensure that intermediate claims are formally auditable. On the balanced WikiArt Influence Benchmark-100 (WIB-100) of 100 artists and 2,000 directed pairs, M-ArtAgent achieves 83.7% positive-class F1, 0.666 Matthews correlation coefficient (MCC), and 0.910 area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (ROC-AUC), with leakage-control and robustness checks confirming that the gains persist when explicit influence phrases are masked. By coupling multimodal perception with domain-constrained falsification, M-ArtAgent demonstrates that implicit influence analysis benefits from historically grounded adjudication rather than pattern matching alone.

摘要：隱含的藝術影響，儘管在視覺上似乎合理，卻常常缺乏文獻記載，因此造成了一個歷史上受限的歸因問題：相似性是必要但不足的證據。大多數先前的系統將影響發現簡化為嵌入相似性或標籤驅動的圖形補全，而最近的多模態大型語言模型（LLMs）仍然容易受到時間不一致性和未經驗證的歸因影響。本文介紹了M-ArtAgent，一個基於證據的多模態代理，將隱含影響的發現重新框架為概率裁決。它遵循一個由調查、證實、反駁和裁決四個階段組成的協議，受一個推理與行動（ReAct）風格的控制器管理，該控制器從圖像和傳記中組裝可驗證的證據鏈，強制執行藝術史公理，並通過一個獨立的批評者對每個假設進行對抗性反駁。兩個基於理論的運算子，StyleComparator用於Wolfflin形式分析，ConceptRetriever用於基於ICONCLASS的圖像學基礎，確保中間聲明在形式上可審計。在平衡的WikiArt影響基準-100（WIB-100）中，包括100位藝術家和2,000對指向性配對，M-ArtAgent達成了83.7%的正類F1、0.666的馬修斯相關係數（MCC）和0.910的接收者操作特徵曲線下面積（ROC-AUC），並且泄漏控制和穩健性檢查確認當顯性影響短語被遮蔽時，增益仍然持續。通過將多模態感知與領域約束的反駁相結合，M-ArtAgent顯示出隱含影響分析受益於歷史上基礎的裁決，而不僅僅是模式匹配。

##### **Cross-Tokenizer LLM Distillation through a Byte-Level Interface**
2604.07466v1 by Avyav Kumar Singh, Yen-Chen Wu, Alexandru Cioba, Alberto Bernacchia, Davide Buffelli

Cross-tokenizer distillation (CTD), the transfer of knowledge from a teacher to a student language model when the two use different tokenizers, remains a largely unsolved problem. Existing approaches rely on heuristic strategies to align mismatched vocabularies, introducing considerable complexity. In this paper, we propose a simple but effective baseline called Byte-Level Distillation (BLD) which enables CTD by operating at a common interface across tokenizers: the byte level. In more detail, we convert the teacher's output distribution to byte-level probabilities, attach a lightweight byte-level decoder head to the student, and distill through this shared byte-level interface. Despite its simplicity, BLD performs competitively with--and on several benchmarks surpasses--significantly more sophisticated CTD methods, across a range of distillation tasks with models from 1B to 8B parameters. Our results suggest that the byte level is a natural common ground for cross-tokenizer knowledge transfer, while also highlighting that consistent improvements across all tasks and benchmarks remain elusive, underscoring that CTD is still an open problem.

摘要：跨標記器蒸餾（CTD），即當教師和學生語言模型使用不同的標記器時，從教師到學生的知識轉移，仍然是一個大多數未解決的問題。現有的方法依賴於啟發式策略來對齊不匹配的詞彙，這引入了相當大的複雜性。在本文中，我們提出了一個簡單但有效的基線，稱為字節級蒸餾（BLD），它通過在標記器之間的共同介面——字節級別上運作來實現CTD。更詳細地說，我們將教師的輸出分佈轉換為字節級概率，將一個輕量級的字節級解碼器頭附加到學生上，並通過這個共享的字節級介面進行蒸餾。儘管其簡單性，BLD在多個基準測試中表現出與顯著更複雜的CTD方法相當的競爭力，並在多個基準上超越它們，涵蓋了從1B到8B參數的多種蒸餾任務。我們的結果表明，字節級別是跨標記器知識轉移的自然共同基礎，同時也強調在所有任務和基準上持續改進仍然難以實現，凸顯出CTD仍然是一個未解決的問題。

##### **Chatbot-Based Assessment of Code Understanding in Automated Programming Assessment Systems**
2604.07304v1 by Eduard Frankford, Erik Cikalleshi, Ruth Breu

Large Language Models (LLMs) challenge conventional automated programming assessment because students can now produce functionally correct code without demonstrating corresponding understanding. This paper makes two contributions. First, it reports a saturation-based scoping review of conversational assessment approaches in programming education. The review identifies three dominant architectural families: rule-based or template-driven systems, LLM-based systems, and hybrid systems. Across the literature, conversational agents appear promising for scalable feedback and deeper probing of code understanding, but important limitations remain around hallucinations, over-reliance, privacy, integrity, and deployment constraints. Second, the paper synthesizes these findings into a Hybrid Socratic Framework for integrating conversational verification into Automated Programming Assessment Systems (APASs). The framework combines deterministic code analysis with a dual-agent conversational layer, knowledge tracking, scaffolded questioning, and guardrails that tie prompts to runtime facts. The paper also discusses practical safeguards against LLM-generated explanations, including proctored deployment modes, randomized trace questions, stepwise reasoning tied to concrete execution states, and local-model deployment options for privacy-sensitive settings. Rather than replacing conventional testing, the framework is intended as a complementary layer for verifying whether students understand the code they submit.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）挑戰傳統的自動程式評估，因為學生現在可以產生功能上正確的程式碼，而不需要展示相應的理解。這篇論文有兩個貢獻。首先，它報告了一項基於飽和度的對話評估方法在程式教育中的範疇回顧。該回顧識別了三個主要的架構類別：基於規則或模板驅動的系統、基於LLM的系統和混合系統。在文獻中，對話代理在可擴展的反饋和深入探究程式碼理解方面顯示出良好的前景，但在幻覺、過度依賴、隱私、完整性和部署限制等方面仍然存在重要的限制。其次，這篇論文將這些發現綜合成一個混合蘇格拉底框架，用於將對話驗證整合到自動程式評估系統（APASs）中。該框架結合了確定性程式碼分析與雙代理對話層、知識追蹤、階梯式提問以及將提示與運行時事實聯繫起來的護欄。論文還討論了針對LLM生成解釋的實際保障措施，包括監考部署模式、隨機追蹤問題、與具體執行狀態相關的逐步推理，以及針對隱私敏感環境的本地模型部署選項。該框架並非取代傳統測試，而是作為一個補充層，用於驗證學生是否理解他們提交的程式碼。

##### **Region-Graph Optimal Transport Routing for Mixture-of-Experts Whole-Slide Image Classification**
2604.07298v1 by Xin Tian, Jiuliu Lu, Ephraim Tsalik, Bart Wanders, Colleen Knoth, Julian Knight

Multiple Instance Learning (MIL) is the dominant framework for gigapixel whole-slide image (WSI) classification in computational pathology. However, current MIL aggregators route all instances through a shared pathway, constraining their capacity to specialise across the pathological heterogeneity inherent in each slide. Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) methods offer a natural remedy by partitioning instances across specialised expert subnetworks; yet unconstrained softmax routing may yield highly imbalanced utilisation, where one or a few experts absorb most routing mass, collapsing the mixture back to a near-single-pathway solution. To address these limitations, we propose ROAM (Region-graph OptimAl-transport Mixture-of-experts), a spatially aware MoE-MIL aggregator that routes region tokens to expert poolers via capacity-constrained entropic optimal transport, promoting balanced expert utilisation by construction. ROAM operates on spatial region tokens, obtained by compressing dense patch bags into spatially binned units that align routing with local tissue neighbourhoods and introduces two key mechanisms: (i) region-to-expert assignment formulated as entropic optimal transport (Sinkhorn) with explicit per slide capacity marginals, enforcing balanced expert utilisation without auxiliary load-balancing losses; and (ii) graph-regularised Sinkhorn iterations that diffuse routing assignments over the spatial region graph, encouraging neighbouring regions to coherently route to the same experts. Evaluated on four WSI benchmarks with frozen foundation-model patch embeddings, ROAM achieves performance competitive against strong MIL and MoE baselines, and on NSCLC generalisation (TCGA-CPTAC) reaches external AUC 0.845 +- 0.019.

摘要：多實例學習（MIL）是計算病理學中用於千兆像素整張幻燈片圖像（WSI）分類的主導框架。<lb/>然而，當前的MIL聚合器將所有實例通過共享路徑進行路由，限制了它們在每張幻燈片固有的病理異質性中專業化的能力。<lb/>專家混合（MoE）方法通過將實例劃分到專門的專家子網絡中提供了一種自然的解決方案；然而，無約束的softmax路由可能導致高度不平衡的利用，其中一個或幾個專家吸收了大部分路由質量，將混合重新壓縮回接近單一路徑的解決方案。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了ROAM（區域圖優化運輸專家混合），這是一種空間感知的MoE-MIL聚合器，通過容量受限的熵最優運輸將區域標記路由到專家池，從而促進平衡的專家利用。<lb/>ROAM在空間區域標記上運作，這些標記是通過將密集的補丁包壓縮成與當地組織鄰域對齊的空間分箱單位來獲得的，並引入了兩個關鍵機制：（i）區域到專家的分配，形式化為具有明確每張幻燈片容量邊際的熵最優運輸（Sinkhorn），在不需要輔助負載平衡損失的情況下強制實現平衡的專家利用；以及（ii）圖正則化的Sinkhorn迭代，將路由分配擴散到空間區域圖上，鼓勵相鄰區域一致地路由到相同的專家。<lb/>在四個WSI基準上進行評估，使用凍結的基礎模型補丁嵌入，ROAM的性能與強大的MIL和MoE基準相當，並且在NSCLC泛化（TCGA-CPTAC）中達到外部AUC 0.845 +- 0.019。

##### **A Systematic Study of Retrieval Pipeline Design for Retrieval-Augmented Medical Question Answering**
2604.07274v1 by Nusrat Sultana, Abdullah Muhammad Moosa, Kazi Afzalur Rahman, Sajal Chandra Banik

Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in medical question answering; however, purely parametric models often suffer from knowledge gaps and limited factual grounding. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) addresses this limitation by integrating external knowledge retrieval into the reasoning process. Despite increasing interest in RAG-based medical systems, the impact of individual retrieval components on performance remains insufficiently understood. This study presents a systematic evaluation of retrieval-augmented medical question answering using the MedQA USMLE benchmark and a structured textbook-based knowledge corpus. We analyze the interaction between language models, embedding models, retrieval strategies, query reformulation, and cross-encoder reranking within a unified experimental framework comprising forty configurations. Results show that retrieval augmentation significantly improves zero-shot medical question answering performance. All experiments were conducted on a single consumer-grade GPU, demonstrating that systematic evaluation of retrieval-augmented medical QA systems can be performed under modest computational resources.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在醫療問題回答方面展現了強大的能力；然而，純粹的參數模型往往存在知識空白和有限的事實基礎。檢索增強生成（RAG）通過將外部知識檢索整合到推理過程中來解決這一限制。儘管對基於RAG的醫療系統的興趣日益增加，但各個檢索組件對性能的影響仍然了解不足。本研究對使用MedQA USMLE基準和結構化教科書知識語料庫的檢索增強醫療問題回答進行了系統評估。我們分析了語言模型、嵌入模型、檢索策略、查詢重構和交叉編碼重排序之間的互動，並在一個包含四十種配置的統一實驗框架中進行。結果顯示，檢索增強顯著提高了零樣本醫療問題回答的性能。表現最佳的配置是使用查詢重構和重排序的稠密檢索，達到60.49%的準確率。專業領域的語言模型在利用檢索到的醫療證據方面也被發現比通用模型更有效。分析進一步揭示了檢索效果與計算成本之間的明顯權衡，較簡單的稠密檢索配置在保持較高吞吐量的同時提供了強勁的性能。所有實驗均在單個消費級GPU上進行，顯示出在適度的計算資源下可以對檢索增強的醫療QA系統進行系統評估。

##### **Joint Optimization of Reasoning and Dual-Memory for Self-Learning Diagnostic Agent**
2604.07269v1 by Bingxuan Li, Simo Du, Yue Guo

Clinical expertise improves not only by acquiring medical knowledge, but by accumulating experience that yields reusable diagnostic patterns. Recent LLMs-based diagnostic agents have shown promising progress in clinical reasoning for decision support. However, most approaches treat cases independently, limiting experience reuse and continual adaptation. We propose SEA, a self-learning diagnostic agent with cognitively inspired dual-memory module. We design a reinforcement training framework tailored to our designed agent for joint optimization of reasoning and memory management. We evaluate SEA in two complementary settings. On standard evaluation with MedCaseReasoning dataset, SEA achieves 92.46% accuracy, outperforming the strongest baseline by +19.6%, demonstrating the benefit of jointly optimizing reasoning and memory. ##### **Validated Intent Compilation for Constrained Routing in LEO Mega-Constellations**
2604.07264v1 by Yuanhang Li

Operating LEO mega-constellations requires translating high-level operator intents ("reroute financial traffic away from polar links under 80 ms") into low-level routing constraints -- a task that demands both natural language understanding and network-domain expertise. We present an end-to-end system comprising three components: (1) a GNN cost-to-go router that distills Dijkstra-quality routing into a 152K-parameter graph attention network achieving 99.8% packet delivery ratio with 17x inference speedup; (2) an LLM intent compiler that converts natural language to a typed constraint intermediate representation using few-shot prompting with a verifier-feedback repair loop, achieving 98.4% compilation rate and 87.6% full semantic match on feasible intents in a 240-intent benchmark (193 feasible, 47 infeasible); and (3) an 8-pass deterministic validator with constructive feasibility certification that achieves 0% unsafe acceptance on all 47 infeasible intents (30 labeled + 17 discovered by Pass 8), with 100% corruption detection across 240 structural corruption tests and 100% on 15 targeted adversarial attacks. End-to-end evaluation across four constrained routing scenarios confirms zero constraint violations with both routers. We further demonstrate that apparent performance gaps in polar-avoidance scenarios are largely explained by topological reachability ceilings rather than routing quality, and that the LLM compiler outperforms a rule-based baseline by 46.2 percentage points on compositional intents. Our system bridges the semantic gap between operator intent and network configuration while maintaining the safety guarantees required for operational deployment.

摘要：操作低地球軌道（LEO）巨型星座需要將高層次的操作員意圖（「將金融流量重新導向至80毫秒以下的極地鏈路」）轉換為低層次的路由約束——這是一項既需要自然語言理解又需要網絡領域專業知識的任務。<lb/>我們提出了一個端到端系統，包含三個組件：<lb/>(1) 一個GNN成本預測路由器，將Dijkstra質量的路由提煉為一個152K參數的圖注意力網絡，實現99.8%的數據包交付率，並達到17倍的推理加速；<lb/>(2) 一個LLM意圖編譯器，使用少量提示和驗證者反饋修復循環，將自然語言轉換為類型約束的中間表示，實現98.4%的編譯率和87.6%在240個意圖基準（193個可行，47個不可行）上的完全語義匹配；<lb/>(3) 一個具有建設性可行性認證的8次通過確定性驗證器，在所有47個不可行意圖（30個標記 + 17個由第8次通過發現）上實現0%的不安全接受率，並在240個結構性腐敗測試中實現100%的腐敗檢測，以及在15個針對性對抗攻擊中實現100%。<lb/>在四個受限路由場景中的端到端評估確認兩個路由器均無約束違規。我們進一步證明，在避免極地的場景中，明顯的性能差距主要是由於拓撲可達性上限而非路由質量解釋的，並且LLM編譯器在組合意圖上比基於規則的基準高出46.2個百分點。我們的系統彌合了操作員意圖與網絡配置之間的語義差距，同時保持了操作部署所需的安全保證。

##### **$k$-server-bench: Automating Potential Discovery for the $k$-Server Conjecture**
2604.07240v1 by Kirill Brilliantov, Etienne Bamas, Emmanuel Abbé

We introduce a code-based challenge for automated, open-ended mathematical discovery based on the $k$-server conjecture, a central open problem in competitive analysis. The task is to discover a potential function satisfying a large graph-structured system of simple linear inequalities. The resulting evaluation procedure is sound but incomplete: any violated inequality definitively refutes a candidate, whereas satisfying all inequalities does not by itself constitute a proof of the corresponding conjecture's special case. Nevertheless, a candidate that passes all constraints would be strong evidence toward a valid proof and, to the best of our knowledge, no currently known potential achieves this under our formulation in the open $k=4$ circle case. As such, a successful candidate would already be an interesting contribution to the $k$-server conjecture, and could become a substantial theoretical result when paired with a full proof.
  Experiments on the resolved $k=3$ regime show that current agentic methods can solve nontrivial instances, and in the open $k=4$ regime they reduce the number of violations relative to existing potentials without fully resolving the task. Taken together, these results suggest that the task is challenging but plausibly within reach of current methods.
  Beyond its relevance to the $k$-server community, where the developed tooling enables researchers to test new hypotheses and potentially improve on the current record, the task also serves as a useful \emph{benchmark} for developing code-based discovery agents. In particular, our $k=3$ results show that it mitigates important limitations of existing open-ended code-based benchmarks, including early saturation and the weak separation between naive random baselines and more sophisticated methods.

摘要：我們介紹了一個基於代碼的挑戰，旨在自動化、開放式的數學發現，該挑戰基於 $k$-server 猜想，這是一個競爭分析中的核心未解問題。<lb/>這項任務是發現滿足大量圖結構的簡單線性不等式系統的潛在函數。<lb/>結果評估程序是健全但不完整的：任何被違反的不等式都明確駁斥了一個候選者，而滿足所有不等式本身並不構成對相應猜想特例的證明。<lb/>儘管如此，通過所有約束的候選者將是有效證明的強有力證據，據我們所知，當前已知的潛在函數在我們的開放 $k=4$ 圓形案例下並未達到這一要求。<lb/>因此，一個成功的候選者將已經是對 $k$-server 猜想的有趣貢獻，並且當與完整證明結合時，可能成為一個重要的理論結果。<lb/>在解決的 $k=3$ 環境下的實驗顯示，當前的代理方法可以解決非平凡的實例，而在開放的 $k=4$ 環境下，它們相對於現有潛在函數減少了違反的次數，但並未完全解決任務。<lb/>綜合這些結果表明，這項任務具有挑戰性，但可能在當前方法的可達範圍內。<lb/>除了對 $k$-server 社群的相關性外，所開發的工具使研究人員能夠測試新的假設並可能改善當前紀錄，這項任務還作為開發基於代碼的發現代理的有用 \emph{基準}。<lb/>特別是，我們的 $k=3$ 結果顯示，它減輕了現有開放式基於代碼的基準的重要限制，包括早期飽和和天真的隨機基線與更複雜方法之間的弱分離。

##### **LaScA: Language-Conditioned Scalable Modelling of Affective Dynamics**
2604.07193v1 by Kosmas Pinitas, Ilias Maglogiannis

Predicting affect in unconstrained environments remains a fundamental challenge in human-centered AI. While deep neural embeddings dominate contemporary approaches, they often lack interpretability and limit expert-driven refinement. We propose a novel framework that uses Language Models (LMs) as semantic context conditioners over handcrafted affect descriptors to model changes in Valence and Arousal. Our approach begins with interpretable facial geometry and acoustic features derived from structured domain knowledge. These features are transformed into symbolic natural-language descriptions encoding their affective implications. A pretrained LM processes these descriptions to generate semantic context embeddings that act as high-level priors over affective dynamics. Unlike end-to-end black-box pipelines, our framework preserves feature transparency while leveraging the contextual abstraction capabilities of LMs. We evaluate the proposed method on the Aff-Wild2 and SEWA datasets for affect change prediction. Experimental results show consistent improvements in accuracy for both Valence and Arousal compared to handcrafted-only and deep-embedding baselines. Our findings demonstrate that semantic conditioning enables interpretable affect modelling without sacrificing predictive performance, offering a transparent and computationally efficient alternative to fully end-to-end architectures

摘要：預測無約束環境中的情感仍然是以人為中心的人工智慧中的一項基本挑戰。雖然深度神經嵌入主導當代方法，但它們往往缺乏可解釋性，並限制了專家驅動的精煉。我們提出了一個新穎的框架，使用語言模型（LMs）作為手工製作的情感描述的語義上下文調節器，以建模情感的價值和喚醒的變化。我們的方法從可解釋的面部幾何和基於結構化領域知識衍生的聲學特徵開始。這些特徵被轉換為符號自然語言描述，編碼其情感含義。一個預訓練的LM處理這些描述，以生成語義上下文嵌入，這些嵌入作為情感動態的高級先驗。與端到端的黑箱管道不同，我們的框架在利用LM的上下文抽象能力的同時，保持特徵的透明性。我們在Aff-Wild2和SEWA數據集上評估所提出的方法，以預測情感變化。實驗結果顯示，與僅使用手工製作和深度嵌入基準相比，對於價值和喚醒的準確性都有持續的改善。我們的研究結果表明，語義調節使得可解釋的情感建模成為可能，而不犧牲預測性能，提供了一種透明且計算效率高的替代方案，取代完全端到端的架構。

##### **Self-Discovered Intention-aware Transformer for Multi-modal Vehicle Trajectory Prediction**
2604.07126v1 by Diyi Liu, Zihan Niu, Tu Xu, Lishan Sun

Predicting vehicle trajectories plays an important role in autonomous driving and ITS applications. Although multiple deep learning algorithms are devised to predict vehicle trajectories, their reliant on specific graph structure (e.g., Graph Neural Network) or explicit intention labeling limit their flexibilities. In this study, we propose a pure Transformer-based network with multiple modals considering their neighboring vehicles. Two separate tracks are employed. One track focuses on predicting the trajectories while the other focuses on predicting the likelihood of each intention considering neighboring vehicles. Study finds that the two track design can increase the performance by separating spatial module from the trajectory generating module. Also, we find the the model can learn an ordered group of trajectories by predicting residual offsets among K trajectories.
